  window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function(){

    $('.box-country-selector.from-left.is-fixed.flyout-container').addClass('initialized');
$('.header-trigger').click(function(){
$('.box-country-selector.from-left.is-fixed.flyout-container, .flyout-cover, body').toggleClass('is-flyout-open');

  $('.flyout-cover').toggleClass('is-fixed');

});
$('.custom-flyout .close, .flyout-cover').click(function(){

  $('.box-country-selector.from-left.is-fixed.flyout-container, .flyout-cover, body').removeClass('is-flyout-open');

  $('.flyout-cover').removeClass('is-fixed');
})    
  })
